< Review>
I really like this dental office. I used to take child to Dental Funzone prefer this place a million times better. An assistant takes in the kid for xrays and the kids stays in the same room throughout the visit, generally tended to by only one assistant. The back office assistants are very nice, cheerful, and friendly. The front office usually isn’t so but there was improvement at my last visit. One thing I wish they would change is remove the carpet from the operatories. It’s pretty unhygienic to not be able to easily mop and disinfect areas where bodily fluids, blood, and other mouth debris fly around in the air on a daily basis. Other than that, though, great service and good location with plenty of parking.</Review>

It’s another boba time outlet. They have a decent selection of teas with choice of boba. Also they have smoothies, shakes and frappe drinks. It is a good choice for afternoon breaks and dessert drinks. Plenty of free parking on the strip mall. < Review>
This review is based solely on two visits in July 2020. It's Boba Time is serious about reducing the spread of COVID. First, there is no indoor or outdoor seating, only take out. Second, every employee wears a mask, and you must wear one yourself to enter. Third, only one patron is allowed in the store at a time, with the queue continuing outside. Fourth, there are plastic shields that cover almost the entire counter. Fifth, cash is not allowed and the staff requires you to wipe down your credit card before handing it to them. So yes, It's Boba Time is taking COVID seriously, and they should be recognized for it.</Review>

< text>
The drinks here are decent, but it can be challenging to find a place to sit here (especially on evenings and on the weekends). There aren't too many tables inside, and there a few outside. There is one big table inside (which I think could seat up to around eight people, but the rest are smaller tables). Given that there is typically a crowd (at least, when I visit), I would not recommend this place for quiet studying. Most of the customers seem to be around the age of college students or twenty-somethings. The workers are nice for the most part, and I haven't had to deal with any unpleasant people behind the counter... which is good! Parking can be a challenge when the whole plaza is busy. It's Boba Time is an OK place to enjoy drinks with a smaller-sized group.< /text>

<Pictures>None</Pictures>< Text>
This place deserves 5 stars. I agree that they can get very busy and crowded.. but its HELPFUL NICE Staff, wide selection and late hours makes it all worth it to drive here for your boba (or shaved ice, desserts, all the good stuff!).
Last week, I lost our debit card on our way there and they helped right away to search for it...once checked and found nothing: got our contact info in case something shows up. The Asian girl at the counter was genuinely friendly; she's the one who personally helped me and asked her colleagues. Very fortunately indeed, we found our card after that visit that apparently just fell out of me before getting to the store..I've let them know this on my comeback visit tonight and saw the girl and we're just both thankful that it's found!
They are empathetic and really good people. I also like one of the shift leads that made up for that night when they unexpectedly lost boba after we placed the order. THIS IS THE PLACE ONE WOULD WANT TO COME BACK TO, again and again.
Personally we never had to wait super long for our drinks, so maybe those were extraordinary busy times what the other reviewers wrote...In any case, what counts is the Service, Authenticity and Smiles of its staff helping you with their wonderful drinks (boba is perfectly chewy, yummiee) -this, my friend, is priceless. Thank you Boba Time.</Text>

<text>Clean, authentic decor, pleasant setting, friendly waitresses, spicy authentic Hunan flavors!  Mapo tofu, walnut shrimps and Special Seethed Fish to die for ... at a very amazing price and generous portion.

The best Spicy Food Restaurant in Southern California in the Valley rivaling Z&Y in Chinatown San Francisco. Gotta try this, feel really cleansing after dining here! The restaurant interior decor is NOT the usual tacky Chinese, this one is tastefully done however simple though not fancy at all.  The outside restaurant front is part of a plaza difficult to enter from freeway 60 exit though parking is plenty and very practical as it is right in front of the restaurant. <Pictures>None< /Pictures><text>Yunnan Garden is seriously one of my favorite restaurants. I make it a point to visit it every so often, if not just for takeout. Everyone I have brought and recommended here has become a regular.

It's the kind of place where you gotta go with someone who knows the ropes. Not everything here is authentically delicious, but if you know what to order, you'll leave one happy customer.

You can't go wrong with any of the cold dishes up front. It's 3 for $5.50. I usually order the pig ears (not spicy) and tofu, and save the 3rd for whatever else I feel like that particular day. Everything made day of so it's super fresh, but beware, they'll run out at the end of the night of the popular ones!

As for dishes, the Water Boiled items are the BEST in the 626. I also regularly order the Pork with Garlic Sauce*, Fried Chicken, Cumin Lamb and Spicy Wontons.

Still need help ordering? I'm available for hire, lunches and dinners :)

*garlic makes the world go 'round</text><Rate>5</Rate>< Response>

< review>
Very well managed fast food hibachi restaurant.

Although there were 7 people working in a tight space, they operated like a well oiled machine.

Two ladies up front did an excellent job controlling the flow of customers.

My food came out very quickly although there were tons of customers there.

I ordered fried rice but they ran out of it. The lady up front (titha?) quickly recognized it and offered me a side of noodles.  Although it costed them nothing to give me the side for free, they earned my business today and in the future.

My experience today was way beyond what I would have expected at a fast food restaurant.</review>

Their sushi is delicious and so cheap! I love the vegetarian options. I haven't found anywhere else that has a vegetable dragon roll. The quality is awesome for the price. They constantly have monthly specials, too, so you can get some rolls or plenty of sides for as cheap as 2 for $5.

We love this place and go here all the time.</Text>

<Pics>None<//Pics>< review>
My first time here and I have to say it's surprisingly good for what is essentially a fast food place.  :)
Prices are very good ( 8 piece roll for $7.95!) and was quite tasty.
Really liked how they listened and didn't put cucumber ( which makes me VIOLENTLY ill) in the rolls, unlike many other Sushi places.
2 blocks south of where Hesperian crosses 92. Free parking, but not a lot.  But there is more around the corner.
Will definitely come here again!
They have shades they roll down when the sun hits the windows, which is AWESOME and keeps it cool and shady.  :)</review>

Place is clean, right off freeway, fast. I got the loin king and Cali roll combo. Great deal at $13.50, but I think the rolls are already pre-made. Usually I wait 15 minutes for a lion king roll, my order was ready in 5 minutes. It was still fresh, but not hot or fresh out the oven & there was a bit too much teriyaki sauce on top, too sweet. The chicken teriyaki comes with rice & steamed veggies, price is good too. But I think I'll ask for less teriyaki sauce, it's really saucy. If you come earlier, they have a BOGO deal, if you're getting 2 orders of teriyaki. They also have deals on the sushi rolls. My rating is 3-1/2 stars.<//Review>

<userid>106359794720120539832<//userid><GmapID>0x808f916287b06c81:0xcf9e36f58428d329</GmapID>< Name>
Think Outside Your Boundaries</Name>
< text>
This is a great place if you want some fast teriyaki foods or rolls. It's kind of a fast food place for Japanese food. Taste-wise, the kids like most of the stuff, however they eat a lot of Japanese foods and still like the traditional sit down restaurants and would rather wait a bit for better tasting dishes.  They said the rice in rolls was on the hard side a d did not have enough vinegar. For the tempura items, the oil seemed a bit old and in need of change.

Pros: free parking; fast service; ample tables to sit at, but most people buy and go, store is pretty clean, and well lit; servers are friendly, and helpful (even making a special roll that was not on their menu; fish and meats are fresh; portions for the numbered combo are very big and one order can feed two; they also have a rewards program (ask about it, i.e. buy ten lion king rolls and get one free)

Cons: very limited open spaces, especially when the other stores next door are open; smoke fills up the restaurant; rolls don't have an authentic taste (fills the stomach and good, but flavor, size, and taste a little different); rice was a little harder than we liked it

We come here a few times a year, and it's best to keep it that way.  It's good when we need something fast.< /text>
